I sincerely recommend friends who travel to Xi'an to stay in this hotel, which may give you a refreshing experience of the InterContinental brand.

msg:First of all, let me declare: I am not a bastard, this review is my most real feeling after leaving the store.

The InterContinental Hotel is located in China Airlines, which is about 40 minutes away from the airport. There are two staff members who maintain order and guide vehicles from the hotel gate to the road about 100 meters away.

The lobby is equipped with two front desks. A greeter is waiting to open and close the door. There is also a floor guide at the radio station. The lobby manager assists on the first floor around the clock. On the right is the restaurant and the swimming pool on the fourth floor, which is not open. The 19th floor lounge is also equipped with a staff member for greeting and registration.

Let‚Äôs talk about the room:
Advantages: They are all equipped with bathtubs, double-layer electric curtains, one upper and one blackout curtain, and one left and one right screen window. The floor is high, so the lighting is great and the view is unobstructed. The bathroom is separated from wet and dry, and the bathtub and bed are separated by a sliding door. The bedding is also good. Double bedding is also provided for single occupancy. A double sofa and a round table serve as a dining table and office. The welcome fruits are changed daily. It gives you the illusion that the president wakes up slowly in his luxurious high-rise hotel and opens the curtains overlooking the city to soak up the sunshine. The air conditioner quilt is a bit thin hahahaha
Breakfast time is from 6 to 10 o'clock. The breakfast supply is very good, including Xi'an-style noodles, Chinese and Western food, fruits, juices, soy milk. I recommend millet porridge and tea eggs, which taste just right.
I woke up late the next day, and it was already half past nine when I came downstairs. The staff gently reminded me that food should be collected at ten o'clock. I drank a bowl of porridge and drank two sugar oranges and a pear.

It‚Äôs 1932 kilometers from Quanzhou to Xi‚Äôan. I got used to the temperature in Quanzhou, but I‚Äôm a little uncomfortable arriving in Xi‚Äôan. The nasal cavity is a bit dry, and the wind is cold rather than wet. So friends from the south who come to Xi‚Äôan remember to wear down jackets with hats. It‚Äôs a breeze to open and close the hotel door. It was the temperature of two worlds. It was 10 o'clock and I couldn't sleep because my nose was bloody. I asked the front desk for a humidifier. The hotel was very considerate and gave me a humidifier and six bottles of water. I commend the hotel for their care. Beach kids are really not used to the winter climate üòÇ

Disadvantages: Non-smoking is allowed on all floors. The hotel entrance is on the far left. The smoking area is set up outside the hotel. There is a small ashtray on the reception desk. As a guest, when I came back from going out, I turned left when I walked to the door. I had to put it out. If you smoke, you must first look for a trash can at the door to extinguish the cigarette. The small ashtray is on the far right, so there may be a blind spot. I have already responded to this problem on the spot, and the hotel handles feedback very quickly. I called the phone as soon as I entered the room. It rang, and the feedback was given to me. The management will make guidelines for smoke extinguishing signs. Full marks for service speed and attitude.
However, the wet and dry bathroom and toilet are separated and there is no exhaust fan? The exhaust fan and air conditioning vents are above the sofa by the window! I looked at the bathroom, and there was only a small, round one with no equipment and no switch. There might be a smell when using the toilet. The sliding door can isolate the smell, but there is no exhaust valve. Once the exhaust door is opened, the smell might be there. I rushed out, but I can praise the small details of the sliding door for buffering. It only needs a slight pull and the door will slowly close. The bathroom has a zero-cold water drain pipe, which is ready for use. However, after taking a bath, the water vapor cannot be drained out or it drains very slowly.

As mentioned above, InterContinental's services and facilities are no worse than those of other hotels, and it has indeed worked diligently to provide the services that a star-rated hotel should have. I am very happy. I personally think it can be compared to "Haidilao" in the accommodation industry. "
Finally, I wish InterContinental Xi'an Hi-tech Hotel business is prosperous!

At the same time, on behalf of Fujian, I would like to welcome all colleagues from InterContinental Hotels and the people of Xi'an to Quanzhou, the Maritime Cultural Silk Road, to experience half the city's fireworks and half the city's fairyland!
